< Review>
The Fred Steak from Schaub's is a local institution. It's so go in fact that it surpasses the steaks at most of the local restaurants but you can only buy it here. The recipe is a secret and the copy cats aren't close.

The steak is jet black and not very appealing, for me that's half the fun, shocking guests with such an unappetizing piece of meat. Any concerns they might have had disappear the moment they taste it however.

Guests from out of town now request the Fred Steak when they visit because it is such a treat.< /Review>

<Name>IntrovertGamer<//Name>< Text>
Harbor barber use to be a place to get great haircuts for a cheap price. Not anymore. The last couple of times I have been here, I have left completely disappointed and shocked by the horrible quality of my haircut. I've been coming here for 9 years. It's strange that the service and quality of the haircuts has declined over time here. The best barbers who use to work here have left to other locations. Most of the barbers who remained are a complete joke to the profession, and they don't seem to care about the quality of their work, and they don't seem to care if they get repeat customers. Half of the barbers just stand around all day and don't do anything. Just talk on the phone or watch TV. Yet, when they get a customer they cut hair as fast and as badly as they possibly can. Seeing how some of these barbers have been here for a couple of years, the horrible quality of their haircuts can't be excused by inexperience. They cut your hair terribly on purpose, or they're really just that bad. I don't know which is worse. There's probably two good barbers left. You'll be able to tell which ones they are because everyone who comes in waits for them and only for them. If you can't tell who the good barbers are just ask someone who is waiting. Everyone else here who cuts hair is not worth the money or the headache. For those that say "you get what you pay for". There's better locations out there, who charge the same or a little bit more. Do your research and GO ANYWHERE ELSE. YOU'VE BEEN WARNED. Most of my friends stopped coming here a long time ago and started going to better places that charge more. I guess it's time to follow their lead and finally let go of this place. Like this place has let go of their quality.</Text>

< Review>
Might have found my new favorite milk tea place!!! So many options, I love it. And I love that they sell milk tea and coffee even though I'm not a coffee drinker. It's nice to know the option is there. I ordered their house milk tea and it's exactly how I like it, just the right amount of sweetness. It's "nitro aasaam tea with brown sugar crema". The nitro part intrigued me. Idk what that really means but makes me feel fancy! I also love that they have smoothies and egg puffs. Will have to try next time.

The only downside is that they open at noon. Idk about y'all but I crave milk tea for breakfast, lunch, and dinner. Haha. Very friendly customer service. 10/10 would recommend.<//Review>

<Review>It was an amazing weekend in Napa. We are celebrating our 25 th wedding anniversary and thought of wine and dine date in Napa. The location of the hotel is topnotch. Walks away from bars and restaurants. No driving and get drunken. Ehemmm. Drink responsibly. The staff are friendly and excellent. Notes was John who checked us in. Allowed us yo park our car for about 30 minutes as we settle in our room. Very helpful in directions and cares for our needs. We were upgraded to a junior suite which was sweet making our anniversary well romantic. The surprise of our stay was the breakfast at the hotel. Coffee was excellent. Order the ham sandwich with egg on the famous model bakery english muffin. You got it right Oprah!!!  My wife had the French toast with fruit compote which was so delicious. Rave about it. The room. The best was good to excellent . Pillows ok but less puffy. Linens are immaculately clean. Towels are great and very very good quality. The bathroom fixtures are just modern and chic and may i add very functional. The quality of water was good. Not hard water. Room temperature as always was set to maximum coolness of 65 defrees. Could be better if it were 60 degrees , we used at cool bay area temp. We could hear a bit annoying noise of the fan motor, could be improved. Large television and good channel selections and options. Felt safe. Convenient to shop, dine and drink around. Would definitely come back and spread the word to think it is still Covid season.</Review>< Pictures>

<review>This hotel is located in a great area of downtown Napa! Beautifully decorated inside any out - I'm in love with the decor and feel of this place, farm-style rustic with contemporary elegant amenities. It's very warm, inviting, friendly, and intimate - I love the vibe and the bar in the lobby!

We were greeted with a complimentary glass of delicious red wine and advised that all non alcoholic snacks in the room were complimentary - wonderful touch. The upgraded suite we booked was lovely - separate living room area with a balcony, fridge, TV, and dual sided fireplace. The bedroom had a super soft and comfortable King bed, large soaker tub, and large shower with rain shower head. Loved the mercantile outdoor patio and bar - cozy, outdoor fire, and plenty of seating.

Breakfast in the hotels restaurant - Farmers Table - was delicious. Loved the Brioche French Toast - my only complaint is I wished they included more than 4 because it was a tease... So delicious with just the whip cream. My hubby had the carnivore omlette‚Äã and loved it, I ate some of his potatoes and it was seasoned and cooked perfectly!

<user_name>Fernando Greenway</user_name><date>1552482833144< /date>< rate>
4</rate>
< Text>
When we decided were to stay in Napa for a weekend getaway and this hotel seemed like the perfect location to all the local restaurants, tasting rooms, and local events. The parking is located at the back of the hotel at a public parking garage. If you stay at the hotel just park on the 3rd floor for your overnight stay.

The hotel booking, the onsite communication, check in/check out processes were all so easy and seamless. We had reserved the king bed city view room and were on the 2nd floor right around the corner where the Mercantile Terrace was located. We unfortunately did not get to enjoy the terrace area during our stay, but the area looked really nice and was lively throughout the evening.

The room itself was big, the bathroom was huge, with a rainfall shower, plenty of counter space and amazing marble floors and shower walls.

They offered complimentary beverages (non-alcoholic) and snacks (which were refilled daily). We also had ordered room service breakfast and the order was up and in our room within 20-30mins. The food was also delicious.

All in all, we enjoyed our stay at Andaz and hope to come back in the future.< /Text>

< Text>
Its been a very long time coming writing my review at the Andaz in Napa but I needed to express my experience.

This last Summer (2018) I had the delight of staying at the Andaz Napa. The room, the vibe of the hotel, the amenities and services were by far the greatest I have experienced at any Hotel. I do a lot of traveling for work so i do know a little about Hotels.

This trip however was for leisure, I had the pleasure of proposing to my fiancee the week I stayed here and to say the staff was more than helpful is a huge understatement. They pointed us in the right direction of some awesome wineries, gave us dinner recommendations and upgraded our room mid stay. They had also added a complimentary bottle to celebrate our engagement.

I would highly recommend this hotel for anyone who wants to stay in the area. Wish I could give a higher review but sadly it is not possible.<//Text>

< text>
We loved our stay at the Andaz. It's only about 4 blocks from the city center of Napa, with free parking right behind the hotel which saved us the valet parking fee. Chic hotel with a bar that was banging all the time, multiple food locations attached or nearby, tray of cookies in the lobby, and really friendly staff. Our room was GORGEOUS with a bathtub next to the bed (complete with complimentary bath salts!), a sitting area, and a TV that could swing from the sitting area to the bed area (why haven't more places thought of this?!). The free snacks and drinks were a big plus too on our days of wine tastings. My favorite thing of the whole place, though, was the bed. I have slept in a LOT of hotels and this bed was by far the most comfortable hotel bed I've ever slept in. Soft sheets, perfect mattress... we never wanted to get up. I would say the only downside to the Andaz was that there's no pool. But overall I'd recommend in a heartbeat.<//text>

I'd love to give this place a good review, but they failed before we started....

My husband and I were booked to stay September 8-10. Unfortunately, when the earthquake hit, this was one of the few properties that was closed because of damage. What is bothersome is that we received no notification that the hotel was closed. We found out by chance on Twitter. Had we not seen the list of hotels we would have been left without a reservation for our trip.

To make matters worse, when we called, they offered no assistance on helping us find an alternative and seemed to be only interested in getting us refunded and off the phone as quickly as possible.

I hear they are closed through the end of September. I hope they have contacted other guests. We were lucky enough to get a reservation at another location.

Don 't get me wrong, the earthquake is an unfortunate situation for all of Napa. But this hotel is owned and operated by Hyatt.  An email or call was expected.  They dropped the customer service ball on this one.</review>

We stayed at the Andaz in March of 2013.  Everything from the check in to our check out was a wonderful experience.  We requested a high room, which I had read to do on other reviews, and they were very accommodating.  I had read that some guests didn't like the fact the gym wasn't located in the hotel.  We didn't mind having access to the downtown sports gym next door.  It was a great place to workout!  ...and it's NEXT door!  We loved the atmosphere in the lobby.  There was wine tastings going on, fresh juice in the mornings, a fire to read the paper by and people eating at the farm to table restaurant.  It was the perfect mix of the wine country and city life.  We loved it and thought the location was great... walking distance to Oxbow Market and right across the street from Oenotri, which is a fabulous restaurant!< /Review>
